## Initial Interpretation

### Definitely Built

- Next.js application structure
- API route topology
- Phase 7, 8, 9, and 10 contract/status routes
- Build/deploy pipeline
- Vercel production deployment path
- GitHub commit history
- DEV2 verification workflow

### Needs Manual Review

- Whether AP2 actually executes tasks
- Whether brain routes use real memory or static logic
- Whether owner console has live data
- Whether node registry is real or static
- Whether search/RSS/YouTube routes are connected to real services
- Whether Prisma schema contains meaningful persistent memory tables
- Whether any route performs actual orchestration beyond returning contract JSON

### High-Risk Scaffolding Indicators

- Large number of phase routes
- Static NextResponse.json patterns
- Repeated mutation_allowed: false
- Repeated simulation_only
- Repeated contract_status
- Contract routes without database/tool calls
